 tippaniyan However, apart from these three countries, people belonging to minority communities of any other country will have to pay 10,000 rupees for registration in India and they will have to pay 15,000 rupees if they register from any other place

 com / v7x6g8hfht What is the festival of Vat Savitri and why is it so important
 hindu parampara main striyaan apane pati kii dderghaayu or sukhad vaivaahik jivan ke liye tamaam vrath kaa paalan karti hai
 Vat Savitri fast is also considered to be a big vow to attain good fortune
 vat savitri vrath-katha or isaki mahimaachah jyeshtha krishna amavasya ko manaaya jaataa he
 This time this fast will be done on 25 May
 iske saath satyawan- vitri kii katha judi hui he
 In which Savitri, with his determination and reverence, withdrew the life of Satyavan from Yamaraja
 mahilaayein bhi sankalp ke saath apane pati kii aayu or praan raksha ke liye is din vrath or sankalp leti hai
 By observing this fast, it is a boon to a happy and prosperous couple
 vatsavitri kaa vrath sampoorn parivaar ko ek sutara main baandhe bhi rakhata he
 Why Vatvriksha (banyan) is worshiped - Vat Vriksha (banyan) is considered a Deva tree - Brahma, Vishnu, Mahesh and Savitri also live in the Vat tree - At the end of the Holocaust, Shri Krishna appeared on the leaf of this tree
 Had happened
 - tulsidas ne vatvriksh ko tirthraj kaa kshatra kaha he
 - This tree is not only extremely sacred, but also has a lot of longevity - This tree is worshiped keeping in mind its long age, strength and religious importance - Regarding the environment, this tree is given so much importance
 Pooja Vidhi of Savitri fast - Take bath early in the morning, take a pledge to remain waterless - install the idol of savitri-satyavan and Yamraj under the Vat tree- Maan Worship them in the form of water - put water in the root of the Vat tree, worship the Vat tree with flowers - incense - and confection - keep circling the Vat tree with raw yarn and wrap it in the cotton stem - revolve at least 7 times Do- Listen to the story of savitri-satyawan with soaked gram in your hand- Still wet gram, give some wealth and clothes to your mother-in-law and take her blessing- Eat fasting by eating the vat tree's spring and other special tasks today What to do - Get a banyan plant planted, maharashtra main biemasi samet 10 mahanagarapalikaon kii 3,210 siton ke rujhaan or nattejey aa rahe hai

 isliye kaha ja rahaa he ki shivasena-bijepi donon kii hi saakh daanv par he

 yadi dopaher 3 baje ke rujhaanon par gaur karen to shivasena 92 siton, bijepi 77 siton, emenes 6 siton par aage chal rahi hai

 a Dalit woman sarpanch is sitting on a dharna in Damoh, Madhya Pradesh
 maamla use 15 agast ko panchayat main jhanda fahraane nahin dene kaa he
 According to the woman sarpanch, the state's minister of power Jayant Malaiya and her son are constantly harassing her
 bagaiyr kisi thos jaanch or notice ke use sarpanch ke pad se hataane kii karrwai kii ja rahi he
 At the behest of the minister, the district collector and officials of the panchayat department are embroiling him in legal troubles
 rajya ke vitt mantri par gambhir aropadalit mahila sarpanch nyaay kii maang ko lekar colector daftar ke saamne dharne par baithi hai, wo yahaan se guzarane vaale logon ko bataati hai ki chaahe rajya kii sarkaar ho yaa centre kii donondaliton ke utthanaki baat karti he, lekin hakeekat bilkul ulti he
 The woman sarpanch sitting on the dharna is named Poona Bai Ahirwar
 puna bai bandakpur gaanv se chunaav ladakar sarpanch chuni gai hai
 For a year, he has had to struggle a lot about his work in the panchayat
 court ke aadesh ke baavjood niyukti main dereepichley saal 15 agast ko jab usnejhanda fahraaneka elaan kiya to swatantraaa diwas se thik do din pehle yani 13 agast 2015 ko use colector ke aadesh ke baad jhanda fahraane se roak diya gaya
 Poona Bai challenged the collector's order in the commissioner's court
 kareeb saal bhar chali sunwaayee ke baad 21 july 2016 ko kamishnar ne colector ke aadesh ko nirast kar diya or puna bai ko waapas sarpanch ke pad kabiz karne ke liye nirdesh die
 Poona Bai alleges that after the issuance of this order, local MLA and state cabinet minister Jayant Malaiya has become active again and pressurized the administration not to appoint him to the post of sarpanch
 jisase colector ne abtak unki bahaali ke aadesh jari nahin kiye
 Poona wants to hoist the flag on August 15, Bai Poona Bai wants to hoist the flag in the Panchayat Bhavan
 lihaaja wo kamishnar ke aadesh par amal karaane ke liye colector ke daftar ke saamne dharne par baithi hai
 The victim woman sarpanch Poona Bai alleges that the finance minister and her son do not want him to be sarpanch
 puna bai jis bandakpur gaanv kii sarpanch he us gaanv ko saansad prahlaad singh patel ne god liya hua he
 Poona Bai has also complained about the case to the MP
